Equation that governs the temperature distribution through a hollow cylinder wall
The temperature is a function of the position in the wall r
T:=T_i-(T_i-T_o)/ln(r_o/r_i)*ln(r/r_i);

The function is governed by the equation, which must equal zero
f -> t = (d^2*T)/(d*r^2)-1/r*(d*T)/(d*r)
f/t = d2 T
d r2 K 1 d T
r d r
T1:=diff(T,r,r);

!Dette script laver en simpel model med et autogenereret mesh. 
!Modellen underbygger et simpelt analytisk tilfælde og undersøger 
!temperatur distributionen igennem en rør væg
/CLEAR,NOSTART
/TITLE,One-Dimensional Steady State Temperature Analysis Through Cylinder Wall
/PREP7  
!Definere element type og key options
ET,1,PLANE223
!Vælger coupled thermal-structural analyse
KEYOPT,1,1,11
!Vælger plane strain
!KEYOPT,1,3,2
!Vælger plane stress
KEYOPT,1,3,0
!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!
!VÆLG MATERIALE [1-8]
i = 8
!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!
! 8 -> PAI: D = 1630, TC = 385, YM = 11.1, CTE = 16.6 !
!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!
!                   1    2     3    4     5    6     7
!Materialer     = [ PPA  PI    PEI  PEEK  PEKK PPS   PTFE]
!Density        = [ 1.49 1.36  1.37 1.35  1.3  1.37  2.16 ]!*e3 (kg/m3) !Density
!Thermal Cond.  = [ 2.08 0.316 0.34 0.557 0.25 2.14  0.292] (W/m-K)
!Youngs modulus = [14    6.61  7.4  4.22  4.7  4.33  0.599]*e9 (GPA)
!Thermal Expan  = [49.6 37.6  38.2 50.7  39.7 51.8 294    ]*e-6 (mu*m/m-C)
*SET,D,1490,1360,1370,1350,1300,1370,2160,1630
*SET,TC,2080,316,340,557,250,2140,292,385
*SET,YM,14e9,6.61e9,7.4e9,4.22e9,4.7e9,4.33e9,0.599e9,11.1e9
*SET,CTE,49.6e-6,37.6e-6,38.2e-6,50.7e-6,39.7e-6,51.8e-6,294e-6,16.6e-6
!Definere materiale værdier
